  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0c4e70af-015a-4efe-8bcd-a47a7870794b'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText12938699411975808103" style="display:none">Wrong side of the tracks—that’s where Kayla’s life has been. Her only saving grace was her sister, Braylin. When Braylin dies, Kayla goes on a mission to avenge her death.<br /><br />Nick is the mysterious stranger with the alluring devil’s eyes. He is attractive, powerful, and dangerous. If not for her obsession for revenge, Kayla would never dare go near him. To lure Nick into her trap, she has to become what he needs while trying to fight against her growing desires. On a destructive path, Kayla enters a secret world of underground crime.<br /><br />As Kayla falls deeper into Nick’s world, she becomes the target of many enemies, and the only one who can save her is the one she has set out to destroy.</span>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_776019276" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/776019276" />
    <a title="Ivie dan Glokta" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta"><img alt="Ivie dan Glokta" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1441134469p2/9838687.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/776019276?book_show_action=true">Nov 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ivie dan Glokta" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ivie dan Glokta" href="/user/show/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta">Ivie dan Glokta</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18333441-the-devil-s-eyes">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">people you want to torture</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=nuclear-waste">nuclear-waste</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9838687-ivie-dan-glokta?shelf=worst-book-i-have-ever-read">worst-book-i-have-ever-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer776019276" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11910115514576902472">Ladies and gentlemen, allow me to introduce you to the undoubtedly <b>WORST BOOK I HAVE EVER READ</b> in my entire life. <br/><br/>In fact it sucked such colossal ass that I have made two brand new shelves just for this book. The first one would be 'worst book I have ever read' (duh...), and it's not really a shelf. It's in fact.............. a throne. The Devil's Eyes will sit there until I the time some other book surfaces that will be even more idiotic, shallow, stupid, unimaginative, cheesy, vulgar, uninspir</span>
  <span id="freeText11910115514576902472" style="display:none">Ladies and gentlemen, allow me to introduce you to the undoubtedly <b>WORST BOOK I HAVE EVER READ</b> in my entire life. <br /><br />In fact it sucked such colossal ass that I have made two brand new shelves just for this book. The first one would be 'worst book I have ever read' (duh...), and it's not really a shelf. It's in fact.............. a throne. The Devil's Eyes will sit there until I the time some other book surfaces that will be even more idiotic, shallow, stupid, unimaginative, cheesy, vulgar, uninspiring, and all together even more catastrophic than this pathetic prosaic monstrosity that crawled out of the sewers to reach the light of day.<br /><br />It sat on my TBR pile for ages, I added it because I loved the blurb, it sounded so promising. It needs to come with a warning to let you know what exactly is the reader getting himself into. <br /><br />Starts like this:<br /><br />On the very first page of the, you guessed it, the very first chapter, our (let's kid ourselves and call her a heroine, just for laughs) “heroine” visits her sister's grave and after a brief moment and a bunch of flowers an old lady walks by that the “heroine” has never seen before in her life and asks her about the grave. Normal, right?..... Wait for it..... <br /><br />The “heroine” launches herself in a monologue three pages long about how sweet her sister was until she met the wrong man, how she took care of her, bought her books, paid the bills and coddled her, until the previously mentioned wrong man starts abusing her....(mind you, this abuse never happens in front of our “heroine's” eyes, but she is certain it's there), because her sister eventually winds up being a prostitute for the man, doing all sorts of illegal things including drugs, and winds up killing her self.<br /><br />The old lady says one thing down the lines of “Oh how awful, and what did you do?”<br /><br />And we are introduced to another mile long monologue, this one featuring her drunken mother, with the support cast of oversexed stepfathers that burned books on the stake and hunted daily for her virginity, culminating in a battle in witch she was saved by a stranger, a man she never saw before....<br /><br />Dafuq did my eyeballs just witness????? Poor little old lady. There is no taking things back after this point, shit seen cannot be unseen.<br /><br />Of all the possible ways to introduce the back-story, like visiting her sister then having solitary cup of coffee while she takes us down memory lane or something so simple the author chooses her “heroine” to go off rambling about the intimate details of potential sexual abuse, sexual awareness and frustration (she even manages to say how she was dreaming the guy was her boyfriend, and she was jealous of her sister) poverty, oddly- a fondness for books- that got a lot of time in the spotlight, then the new career as a stripper/prostitute to a random stranger over her sister's grave. <br /><br />Moving on:<br /><br />Next chapter gives us the pleasure of our “heroine” starting work as a stripper in an upscale nightclub, so elite and exclusive that only the best, most talented dancers who of course have to be the most beautiful women out there work. Of course, she is one of them, because she is so friggin awesome. Without a doubt her performance outshines everyone else's (naturally). She sets the gears in motion to get her revenge on a man that is such a a hardened criminal, even his shadow is afraid of him. If only she could somehow get his attention....oh my let's just finish our job of getting naked for the guests, then even though we are staff, stroll down and take a seat in front of the VIP area where the evil boss man sits, then take our book out and start reading it, loudly ignoring him......in the middle of the night........in an upscale strip club.......reading a book...... amongst the guests........that just saw you get nekkid............ignoring your boss????<br /><br /><b>BUAAAAAAAAAAAAAHAHAHHAHAAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHA.</b> I never guffawed in my life, but I guffawed when I read that. <br /><br />You don't have to be upscale to know how the staff-guest relations work, but just from that nugget it's painfully obvious that the author and upscale met only on paper. <br /><br />Even further:<br /><br />She finally gets his attention, being so friggin awesome as she is, and he takes her to an auction to see how much money would people bid to shag her. The night ends and he is furious, why??? Because everyone bid on her, all of them solely on her and not a single other woman!! Well we all knew that she is so friggin awesome, looks like he's finally catching on. Good for you, son, now let's get this party started! He takes her to his house, where the most incredibly stupid sex scene happens. He gets hot, they both get naked, then he storms out because he forgot some meeting?!? She falls asleep to be woken by some other guy taking her panties off while her boss watches. She slaps the shit out of the guy, threatens her boss (who is a hardened criminal, murderer,pimp, drug pusher and all that) that she will call the cops on him.<br /><br /><br /><b>BUAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHAHA.</b> Would you look at that? I guffawed twice.<br /><br />Anyhooo she somehow winds up unsexed walking out of his house in his clothes, because she stripped the dress he gave her in her righteous rage. Love this quote:<br /><br /><i>“Leaving his house smelling of him,wearing his clothes and feeling strangely more aware of him then ever before I can't help but wonder... Why didn't he kill me?”</i><br /><br />Bitch, me either. One of the worlds greatest mysteries till this day.<br /><br />Yeah, i know, i know, don't get upset, fictional characters and all that, if this novel was based on any logic and common sense, he would be behind bars and fetured in <i>"The world's dumbest criminals"</i> after all the stupidities he pulled, and she would be dead, because we all know that people can't live without a brain. But still...<br /><br />Now I have only covered a few chapters of this novel and not even touched all the points that were so very wrong with this book. Like the moment he is about to have sex with her and she thinks how the last time she saw him like this with his dick out was when he fucked her sister...awww<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www...what">www...what</a> an emotionally charged moment. *gag* If this book was being reviewed by genuine critics I see the words like brazen and bold coming up. Don't get me wrong it's not the novel itself it's the author. She had an interesting concept but it felt like she was tripping over her own shoes in her hurry to tell her story and wind up with such unbelievable nonsense that is an absolute insult to the readers intelligence. To top all of that, this is only the first book of the series. There are two more. I must congratulate her for sticking up for her work and moving on. She proved that producing something as horrendous as this novel didn't shake her resolve but in fact solidified it. This woman honestly scares me. I am afraid of her.<br /><br />The second shelf I have added for this book would be the 'nuclear waste' shelf, because I firmly believe that any prolonged exposure to Loren's writing would cause hair loss, second and third degree burns, organ failure and culminate in a slow and painful death. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11910115514576902472" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer529392670" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13012265038949116176"> -100 stars, DNF<br/><br/>What a waste of my hard earned cash this was! I can't believe there are readers out there who found this badly written tosh (and 'tosh' is putting it mildly) worth their praise. I have read many an awful book in my time but this has to be the worst, the Everest summit of stinking awful. <br/><br/>Upon reading the synopsis, one is horribly mislead to expect a gritty dark story of two damaged people finding one another while groping through their violent, unyielding world. Well, it is nothin</span>
  <span id="freeText13012265038949116176" style="display:none"> -100 stars, DNF<br /><br />What a waste of my hard earned cash this was! I can't believe there are readers out there who found this badly written tosh (and 'tosh' is putting it mildly) worth their praise. I have read many an awful book in my time but this has to be the worst, the Everest summit of stinking awful. <br /><br />Upon reading the synopsis, one is horribly mislead to expect a gritty dark story of two damaged people finding one another while groping through their violent, unyielding world. Well, it is nothing of the sort. It is a mere concoction of badly written little episodes as they came in and flew straight out of the head of the writer without any effort to put together the semblance of a narrative, let alone create a world, a mood, the feeling of an experience. There was no attempt at setting a pace, and no care for the demands of that thing called narrative flow. All you get for your trouble of reading this pile of rubbish is the flattest, most cardboard cut-out of a heroine, and a zero-dimensional hero (so cardboard and zero-dimensional that calling them stupid would endow them with a depth they lack). <br /><br />I must admit, I did roar with laughter (not what the writer intended to elicit) at the lack of understanding of the most basic, minimal psychology and the complete lack of simple logical connections (I'm not talking about coherence, I won't go all intellectual on you) between the heroine's musings/feelings and her actions, as every eight pages a new man, with a 'secret' agenda, and oodles of priapic lust for the heroine, is introduced into this woman's life and she, who's supposedly deeply, darkly, and fatefully in love with the hero, immediately starts planning a new life with the latest dick on the block. I don't mean wanting to hump him or an one night stand, no, she starts thinking 'relationship material' and plans to set up home with him, choose curtains, go through the Argos catalogue.<br /><br />On and on it went, endless in its repetitious tedium, inexhaustible in its flatness and blind to its own inanity. And as if all those failings were not enough to have this book marked 'return to sender' and never published, the sex scenes are awfully boring too. Unfortunately, I have also bought the sequel to this dross but I shall not be subjecting myself to the torture that is Jennifer Loren's prose any longer. The delete button is my friend.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3706719996174555172">This is like horrible, horrible fanfiction. There were grammar mistakes EVERYWHERE, though they may have fixed it before published. I've only read half of the preview and although I planned to read it all, I just couldn't bring myself to finish it. It wasn't even a story, just a long-winded series of "I hate you. Now fuck me.   <span id="freeText3706719996174555172" style="display:none">This is like horrible, horrible fanfiction. There were grammar mistakes EVERYWHERE, though they may have fixed it before published. I've only read half of the preview and although I planned to read it all, I just couldn't bring myself to finish it. It wasn't even a story, just a long-winded series of "I hate you. Now fuck me. JK, don't touch me, I hate you. No, wait, I've changed my mind, fuck me NOW." Also, there were parts that were extremely vague. It shows that you're too lazy to come up with a creative way to incorporate their background into the story so you just forced it through the characters' mouths. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I highly doubt anyone would explain the history of their past relation with a dead sister to an old lady that they barely know. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Even if being polite. <br /><br /><b>Conclusion:</b><br />If I can barely stomach the preview, how the hell would I handle the book? </span>

its a rollercoaster nail biting heartbreaking hot steamy screamin fustrating mind blowing jaw droping crazy mixed emotions going on in this series!!! but you will love all of it no doubt its not enough you will want more i still do and can not wait for The Devil's Son to come out and The Devil's Masqurade ahhhhhhhhh im still Reeling over these characters i cant stop thinkin bout them im in a slump and need a good fix to get over them ...This series has truley became my top favorite 3 of books omg i love it so much ..please take the time and read itttttttttttttt i promise you'll love it as much !!!         <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer506336548&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer506336548" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer233168894137279471">Kayla`s sister killed herself after her boyfriend/pimp/criminal-psycopath (Nick) dumps her sorry ass. Kayla then sets out to get revenge. Planning to get close enough to kill the guy. Insted of killing him at her first chance, which I would say she could have done a million times, she let`s him be her pimp!!! She wants to prove herself to him by being a good whore. This is real character building, if you ask me?!? Jesus! Then she falls in love with her pimp, because he`s just so freaking good lo</span>
  <span id="freeText233168894137279471" style="display:none">Kayla`s sister killed herself after her boyfriend/pimp/criminal-psycopath (Nick) dumps her sorry ass. Kayla then sets out to get revenge. Planning to get close enough to kill the guy. Insted of killing him at her first chance, which I would say she could have done a million times, she let`s him be her pimp!!! She wants to prove herself to him by being a good whore. This is real character building, if you ask me?!? Jesus! Then she falls in love with her pimp, because he`s just so freaking good looking and treats her like trash. <br />Then we find out he has known who she is the entire time and is desperatly in love with her. That is why he pimps her out, to scare her away! Yes! They are that fucking stupid! I`m not one to preach, but come on!?! Even a pimp must have some standards? Right? Hell, I don`t know..<br />In the beginning plot seemed okay. Pretty soon the it derailed from the "revenge" aspect and spiraled out to a bunch of random events. <br />Now, English is my second language, but still the grammar bothered me. The editing is horrific. Skipping days, months by suddenly summing up what happend in a few short sentences. I feel next to no compassion for the characters. The character building of the boyfriend is really, really bad, I just don`t know the guy. <br />And Kayla is almost raped time and time again, but saved at the last minute by Nick the sweetheart. Every man in this book is pretty much a rapist waiting to happen. Really sexy stuff! To say the characters are one-dimentional is putting it mildly.<br />There are twists and turns in the story, which have no effect because it`s so predictable it is`nt funny! The author takes away from the story by not letting us make the connections. This book has a cliffhanger ending, that again is just too freaking easy. We know he is a live! I mean, really? How stupid do you think we are? For some reason I always finish the book, no matter how bad. Usually I have to finish the series also, but with this one I`m not sure I can. As fanfiction I guess it is what it is, some will probably love it, but I can`t. </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10480068-cece?shelf=mob-mafia">mob-mafia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10480068-cece?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10480068-cece?shelf=amazon-own">amazon-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10480068-cece?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10480068-cece?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10480068-cece?shelf=not-for-me">not-for-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10480068-cece?shelf=read-2013">read-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10480068-cece?shelf=amazon-bought">amazon-bought</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer603985844" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7498899766569108786"><b>09/13/16</b> - OMG What was I thinking or have my reading tastes changed in three years?!?! I originally gave this book 4 stars back in 2013. I started to reread it since I noticed I had book 2 in my TO READ shelf, but I could not remember one thing about the book. So I started it yesterday and I can not believe I was not disturbed the first time. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[The hero, Nick, claims he loves the heroine and has always loved her, but he pimps her to his clients and she becomes a prostitute. One of </span></span>
  <span id="freeText7498899766569108786" style="display:none"><b>09/13/16</b> - OMG What was I thinking or have my reading tastes changed in three years?!?! I originally gave this book 4 stars back in 2013. I started to reread it since I noticed I had book 2 in my TO READ shelf, but I could not remember one thing about the book. So I started it yesterday and I can not believe I was not disturbed the first time. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The hero, Nick, claims he loves the heroine and has always loved her, but he pimps her to his clients and she becomes a prostitute. One of those johns a.k.a. "clients" turn out to be his brother, Daniel. He pimps her to his own brother?!?!? But you do not know he is his brother until much later. At first when I was reading those scenes I thought I was mistaken and went back to reread them, but there is no mistaken what was happening. Then I thought maybe those clients that Nick was giving to the heroine were the ones that only wanted to cuddle or spend time together and not have sex, but that was not the case. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> My rating has changed from 4 to 2 stars. The writing is still good, but what the hero allows to happen, is not love to me. Like I mentioned...what was I thinking 3 years ago?!?!?<br /><br />09/12/16 - I am going to reread this one since I forgot a lot of what was going on and I have book 2 in my TO READ shelf. Right now I am curious why I liked this book so much when the prologue is the hero with the heroine's sister and I have never liked stories about having 'left-overs'. Maybe this book was also my 'out of comfort' read. I try to read those once in awhile since I tend to always read the same type of stories. Well I will find out.<br /><br />05/8/13 - OMG, my stomach is in knots after reading this book. Non-stop action. Not a single dull moment in that book. <br /><br />When I originally saw the cover, I thought that this book was a paranormal. No, it is not a paranormal. No paranormal activity in this book. Nick just has the best eyes…the devil’s eyes.<br /><br />The first couple of chapters I could not believe what was happening. Not your typical love story here and that is what made it all the more interesting. There is no insta-love with this couple. It is honest and no hearts and roses. Well maybe later. This is a crime/mob book with a crime/mob hottie. <br /><br />I was initially so nervous about Nick and what his intentions were. I was not able to relax until in the middle we got Nick’s POV. Wow, the book changed then. Steamy…hot…intense.<br /><br />“I love you. I love you Kayla. I hate it, but I do. You drive me absolutely insane but I love you so much that I think about you constantly. Even when you sleep right next to me, I worry that if I fall asleep that you might not be there when wake up.”<br /><br />Did I skim? No<br /><br />Did I feel connected to the characters? Yes. <br /><br />Pace of the story: Good. Intense.<br /><br />Positives: Great story, great writing. Something is always happening. You do not know where the story is going to take you. I was so nervous. Loved that half way through the book we got Nick’s POV. Those were the best chapters. With chapter, you wil not know where the story is going to go. <br /><br />Negatives: Not sure what my negatives are even days after finishing this book. I was instantly involved in the story and the characters. Do I love Nick? Do I trust Nick? I do but so nervous. He is a crime boss after all. <br /><br />Do I recommend? Yes<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7498899766569108786" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/857461294" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/857461294?book_show_action=true">Feb 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18333441-the-devil-s-eyes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer857461294" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16542459699035271373"><b>4.5 Holy Moly STARS!</b><br/><br/><b>The Devil’s Eyes does not get enough credit! It’s one crazy book with action, romance and secrets. It will leave you shaking once finished.</b><br/><br/>Kayla only has her sister, Braylin. When Braylin commits suicide because of a breakup, it’s Kayla’s mission to avenge her sister’s death. Kayla plans to seduce and hurt Nick, Bryalin’s ex-boyfriend. But Nick is no normal boyfriend, he’s lives a dangerous world that Kayla isn’t afraid to jump in. <br/><br/><b>WHAT A CRAZY STORY?!!!!!!</b><br/><br/>I picked up The Dev</span>
  <span id="freeText16542459699035271373" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Holy Moly STARS!</b><br><br><b>The Devil’s Eyes does not get enough credit! It’s one crazy book with action, romance and secrets. It will leave you shaking once finished.</b><br><br>Kayla only has her sister, Braylin. When Braylin commits suicide because of a breakup, it’s Kayla’s mission to avenge her sister’s death. Kayla plans to seduce and hurt Nick, Bryalin’s ex-boyfriend. But Nick is no normal boyfriend, he’s lives a dangerous world that Kayla isn’t afraid to jump in. <br><br><b>WHAT A CRAZY STORY?!!!!!!</b><br><br>I picked up The Devil’s Eyes because I wanted an action pack book with a damaged Hero and boy did I get that. Kayla is a tough cookie. Her story is very sad. She loved her sister and doesn’t understand why Braylin killed herself. Kayla decides to be a stripper for the club Nick owns. What I love about Kayla is she is no “innocent” girl. She wants to avenge her sister, so she has to be a stripper? Sure! She strips with pride and uses her brain to get Nick’s attention.<br><br>Then she has to become a prostitute! She again, doesn’t bat an eye and this is when I get REALLY into the book. I love leading ladies with sad past, but a strong disposition that isn’t annoying. Kayla isn’t like I-AM-WOMAN-HEAR-ME-ROAR, she simply knows what she needs to do to get the job done. She’s sassy, funny and really smart. I love interaction between the men that cross her path.<br><br>As for NICK, he’s the Hero you love to hate and want to take to bed. He’s a grade-A jerk and not the kind where you understand his actions, oh no, he doesn’t care about anyone but himself. Does he chase after Kayla? No. Does he let her sell her body to other men? Yes. Nick’s character is really interesting to me. He has so much power and it comes with a high price. Nick is untouchable. Although he isn’t overly interested in Kayla, you can tell he keeps his eye on her at least.<br><br>Connor, one of Kayla’s clients gets a little too interested with Kayla and things get really interesting. There is a slight love triangle, but the tension is so high, it’s anything but entertaining. I love the banter and love/hate relationship Kayla and Nick have. I was glued to the pages and couldn’t get enough!<br><br>A lot of obstacles go on in The Devil’s Eyes, there’s NEVER a dull moment. Just think a combination of Killing Sarai and Sempre. It’s just crazy action, suspense and you never know what’s going to happen.<br><br> The ending wasn’t a surprise, but oh by the OPEN CLIFFY will leave you hanging speechless. I enjoyed this book A LOT and I can’t wait for book 2.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18333441.The_Devil_s_Eyes__The_Devil_s_Eyes___1_" title="The Devil's Eyes (The Devil's Eyes, #1) by Jennifer Loren" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1376574718s/18333441.jpg" alt="The Devil's Eyes (The Devil's Eyes, #1) by Jennifer Loren" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B005YFEEU8/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B005YFEEU8&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><br>For more reviews - &gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com">http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16542459699035271373" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Violence, prostitution, betrayal, revenge and that power-struggle-war! With powerful characters at play. It was stunning and shocking... that got me captivated from start to finish.<br/><br/>Kayla though stubborn, she will grow on you... her character is feisty, daring and resilient! I could not believe the length she would go to to achieve what she wants. She definitely shocked me.. Add</span>
  <span id="freeText5203812099309356910" style="display:none"><b>5 Stunning STARS!</b><br><br><br>I don't even know where to begin!!!! I love mafia romance novels and this book takes it up a notch!!!! Violence, prostitution, betrayal, revenge and that power-struggle-war! With powerful characters at play. It was stunning and shocking... that got me captivated from start to finish.<br><br>Kayla though stubborn, she will grow on you... her character is feisty, daring and resilient! I could not believe the length she would go to to achieve what she wants. She definitely shocked me.. Adding to that, the things that she went through, the person she became, for Nick, I'm just stunned!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2jwdtx" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

I could not believe that he would let Kayla go that far to discourage her... knowing his feelings afterwards towards Kayla, I was again shocked and a bit disappointed in line with again just shocked but being the powerful boss of the crazy mafia world, what do I know! Though yes, one twist of the story was predictable, BUT I don't feel like it brought the storyline down, in fact, I was waiting for that climatic scene! And then, there it was! A definitely explosive ending that makes me want to scream and reach for the second book right away!<br><br>This is not a short read... it introduce us to the gangster world where the danger never cease to end. The length you would do, sacrifice you make, to protect the ones you love! <div id="review_544014983" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/544014983" />
    <a title="Jessy (Jessy&#39;s Book Club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13319152-jessy-jessy-s-book-club"><img alt="Jessy (Jessy&#39;s Book Club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1355235843p2/13319152.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/544014983?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessy (Jessy&#39;s Book Club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessy (Jessy&#39;s Book Club)" href="/user/show/13319152-jessy-jessy-s-book-club">Jessy (Jessy&#39;s Book Club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13010456-the-devil-s-eyes">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13319152-jessy-jessy-s-book-club?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13319152-jessy-jessy-s-book-club?shelf=tortured-heroes">tortured-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13319152-jessy-jessy-s-book-club?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13319152-jessy-jessy-s-book-club?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13319152-jessy-jessy-s-book-club?shelf=dark-romance">dark-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer544014983" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer139196414058541562">[Read more reviews at <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://jessysbookclub.wordpress.com'>http://jessysbookclub.wordpress.com</a>]<br/><br/>OMG! Yet another mind fuck! I haven’t had that since the Consequences Series by Aleatha Romig! Romantic Suspense just might be superseding Erotic Romance for my favorite spot!<br/><br/>First a synopsis: Kayla’s older sister Bray is the only family she has. Bray is the perfect older sister, working hard to get her little sister to college. That’s until she meets Nicholas Jayzon. Everything in Bray’s life spirals out of control until one day Kayla fi</span>
  <span id="freeText139196414058541562" style="display:none">[Read more reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jessysbookclub.wordpress.com">http://jessysbookclub.wordpress.com</a>]<br /><br />OMG! Yet another mind fuck! I haven’t had that since the Consequences Series by Aleatha Romig! Romantic Suspense just might be superseding Erotic Romance for my favorite spot!<br /><br />First a synopsis: Kayla’s older sister Bray is the only family she has. Bray is the perfect older sister, working hard to get her little sister to college. That’s until she meets Nicholas Jayzon. Everything in Bray’s life spirals out of control until one day Kayla finds her dead. Determined to get revenge, Kayla works up a plan and gets a job working as a stripper in Nicholas’ club. Nicholas is gorgeous, has every woman eating out of his hand, but he’s also involved in very criminal activities. Kayla knows just how to get to him, that’s if she doesn’t end up like all the other women…<br /><br />I got this one from a Goodreads friend’s Favorites Bookshelf. Every recommendation I pick up from her shelf is always a 4 or 5 star read so I was very excited for this one. That was until I started it, it gave a whole new meaning to lowering your expectations. I was so disappointed by what I can only describe as grammatical inconsistencies. I felt like the author had not really decided which tense to write the book in. That actually really bothered me. I went back to Goodreads and I couldn’t believe all the raving reviews! Made me re-check whether I bought the right book!<br /><br />At about 30% things look up a bit. I will guiltily admit that it’s no coincidence that I started enjoying it just when the book started steaming up ;)But that’s not all, though the writing still felt weird to me, it started becoming more like background noise. At 50% I was still tempted to let this one go (a true testament to my indecisive nature) but then we got Nick’s POV! It was so sweet and surprising better written (or maybe by this point I had gotten used to the writing). Either way I stopped debating whether to give up on the book. <br /><br />At 60% I became glad I stuck it out! Its not just the relationship that develops between Nick and Kayla (I of course loved the steamy scenes) but you get drawn into this undercover criminal world that is complex and disturbing, yet you get so caught up, its like pure adrenalin rush! Nick was such an asshole in the beginning, he treated Kayla so badly I wondered if he’d ever redeem himself. But then he does and he becomes just perfect in my opinion…well as perfect as a criminal can be…<br /><br /><b>“I want you to come home with me.” He says cradling me and sighing as he leans his head against mine. “Come home with me Kayla. I want you … back in my bed, my house … my life.”</b><br /><br />And then as if that isn’t enough, the stakes go higher. See, Nick’s dealings have made him countless enemies. He’s not only wanted by the cops, he also has rivals to deal with. And this all just escalates. I think I read the last 20% with my jaw on the ground. The drama, the secrets being slowly revealed… I actually re-read some scenes fearing I would miss something vital to the story. And then the end! Is it possible for eyes to water in shock? Mine did! I think I was relieved and shocked at the same time which trust me is a weird feeling!<br /><br />Now I HAVE to get the sequel!<br /><br />The first half of the book is a 2 star but the second half is a definite 4 star! So let’s settle for what? 3 star? Maybe 3.5…gah! I’ll rate it when I’ve calmed down!</span>
  <a data-text-id="139196414058541562" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer322052784" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8006553117658504161">Deny it all u want, everyone loves a bad boy & Nick is as bad as they come! Love him!! But seriously, awesome book. Pulled me in and didnt let go. Lots of action & superhott chemistry!! Kept me on the edge of my seat. I would have liked to see more from Nicks POV though, I liked getting into his head. It made u realize that no matter how badly he treated Kayla sometimes u saw where he was coming from & loved him more for it. It was also refreshing to see Kaylas transformation thru-out the book. </span>
  <span id="freeText8006553117658504161" style="display:none">Deny it all u want, everyone loves a bad boy &amp; Nick is as bad as they come! Love him!! But seriously, awesome book. Pulled me in and didnt let go. Lots of action &amp; superhott chemistry!! Kept me on the edge of my seat. I would have liked to see more from Nicks POV though, I liked getting into his head. It made u realize that no matter how badly he treated Kayla sometimes u saw where he was coming from &amp; loved him more for it. It was also refreshing to see Kaylas transformation thru-out the book. She wasnt ur typical heroine waiting around to be rescued all the time, she really came into her own &amp; took to her new unexpected life better then anyone would have thought. Plenty of twists &amp; turns &amp; OMFG moments thinking who the hell can I trust!! The only complaint I have is the ending, CliffHangers drive me INSANE!!! I will be not-so-patiently climbing the walls til the next book comes out!! Jennifer Loren has definitly landed on my favs list &amp; I CANNOT wait to see what she comes out with next =] </span>
  <a data-text-id="8006553117658504161" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer681354903" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18332778365209788383">If you had asked me to rate this when I was at 50% of this book I would have given it 1 star. I actually almost stopped reading around that point and was thinking it was about a 1 star read. The first half was written almost like a 3rd grader had written it. I am not a grammar/punctuation nazi at all. I feel like a book should be rated on the story, characters, and delivery unless the grammatical errors are so bad that I can't understand the book. This writing was awful during the first half of </span>
  <span id="freeText18332778365209788383" style="display:none">If you had asked me to rate this when I was at 50% of this book I would have given it 1 star. I actually almost stopped reading around that point and was thinking it was about a 1 star read. The first half was written almost like a 3rd grader had written it. I am not a grammar/punctuation nazi at all. I feel like a book should be rated on the story, characters, and delivery unless the grammatical errors are so bad that I can't understand the book. This writing was awful during the first half of the book. Some points of the story were rushed and the characters were one dimensional. Also the hero Nick is not what I expected or wanted in the male lead. He was a pimp and a mobster which I have no problem with. He possessively has such undying love for Kayla that he has been in love with her since they were teens. The funny thing is and where this book loses me is when he hires her as a stripper in his club and even goes as far as pimping her out. One of the people he pimped her out too was his own brother btw but apparently he was using an assumed name so he didn't know this. I just don't think that someone who's hopelessly in love with Kayla would have pimped her out and pushed her into prostitution.Normally anti-heroes are some of my favorites. I really like some of the mobsters and gangsters in lead roles in books. They just usually treat their women a lot different then Nick did. Something happens midway through this book and I'm not sure why. It's almost like one person wrote the first half and a totally different author wrote the second half of this book. Everything about it is different. The writing style, the characters reactions even. Nick goes from pimping her out to being a possessive alpha male. It was totally weird. IMO this book was not worth the $3 it cost in kindle edition.The first half especially read like a bad fan fiction. I will say that the premise and the second half of the story was really good. Someone could rewrite this book and make it great. I liked who Kayla and Nick were during the second half of the book and I loved them fighting/hating one another during the first half. I just didn't like Nick's inconsistent behavior and Kayla being a whore. It didn't jive with the rest of the book. I also refuse to like this series if Kayla gets with Ryan. Really do they have to continue to sleep with one anther's siblings? Ugggghhhh</span>
  <a data-text-id="18332778365209788383" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7931646535756779590">What in God's name was this?<br/>Did I even read the same book as all this 5 star reviewers?<br/>Amazon, you sold me the broken copy and I want my damn money back!<br/>Or am I just too old for this s*it?! </span>

<div id="review_537813222" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537813222" />
    <a title="Triin from T&#39;s Bookish Moments" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4483565-triin-from-t-s-bookish-moments"><img alt="Triin from T&#39;s Bookish Moments" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1359290785p2/4483565.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/537813222?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Triin from T&#39;s Bookish Moments" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Triin from T&#39;s Bookish Moments" href="/user/show/4483565-triin-from-t-s-bookish-moments">Triin from T&#39;s Bookish Moments</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4483565-triin-from-t-s-bookish-moments?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4483565-triin-from-t-s-bookish-moments?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4483565-triin-from-t-s-bookish-moments?shelf=mafia">mafia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537813222" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6973090125747154643">From <a href='http://tsbookishmoments.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>my blog</a>.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>Nicholas Jayzon commanded attention when he walked into a room. If you were ever damned enough to make eye contact with him, you would know what it is like to be lured in by The Devil’s Eyes. </i>
</b><br/><br/>I definitely have a weakness for well-written mafia romances like Crow's Row (I'm still waiting for the second book...) and the Untouchable series, and this is right next to my all-time favorites. It had the right balance of romance, steamy scenes and suspense, and kept me on my toes the en</span>
  <span id="freeText6973090125747154643" style="display:none">From <a href="http://tsbookishmoments.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">my blog</a>.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Nicholas Jayzon commanded attention when he walked into a room. If you were ever damned enough to make eye contact with him, you would know what it is like to be lured in by The Devil’s Eyes. </i>
</b><br /><br />I definitely have a weakness for well-written mafia romances like Crow's Row (I'm still waiting for the second book...) and the Untouchable series, and this is right next to my all-time favorites. It had the right balance of romance, steamy scenes and suspense, and kept me on my toes the entire night. <br /><br />I can't even say how much I enjoyed this book. I had just begun reading The Education of Sebastian and I liked it well enough, but I had been feeling restless for the entire day and that story just wasn't fast enough for me. I just took a quick look at Goodreads and I'm not even sure where I saw the cover of this book and the rating (it was something like 4.3 out of 5). I read the blurb and I just knew I needed this book right away. I have never done a better decision.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Nick has a reputation and every woman in the city is aware of it, if not from word of mouth, then simply by catching a glimpse of him.</i>
</b><br /> <br />I was taken with Nick the first time we saw him and the infatuation just continued to grow throughout the book. He is the definition of a bad boy and I so, so, so love a good bad boy (LOL). I mean, it can't really get any badder that a cold-hearted mafia boss, right? He has this presence that just draws people to him and makes them scared of him at the same time. He's cold and calculating and doesn't seem to care about anyone else but himself. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Come on Nick, did you have parents or did the devil just create you from some spare parts?”</i>
</b><br /><br />Kayla's sister was one of his conquests and she's looking for revenge. She's spent years studying him and she's ready to beat him at his own game. She gets herself hired as a dancer in one of his clubs to get closer to him. She has a plan to kill him and doesn't really care about anything else because she has nothing to lose. Kayla's strong and smart and resourceful. She had the worst childhood, but she's grown into a wonderful young woman. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Wine?” He asks while already perusing the wine list. <br />“Sure. If you’re buying, I will have one of each.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Nick and Kayla are really similar and get into way too many arguments. Plus, she tries to kill him... While she may try to be immune to his charm and his eyes, she never really is (I mean, she does fall in love with the devil...). I really, really enjoyed watching her take control over him and I loved how deep in love the devil fell. And here's another reason I love mafia romances: the guy would anything to keep his girl alive and well; there are are no laws in this world, which also means there are no limits how far he can gp. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Go clean yourself up and go to bed. You don’t have to go to sleep and you can go to bed with your bat, if you like, but the quicker you look vulnerable, the quicker they will try to kill you.” <br />“Oh, well. Let me hurry then.” I said faking my excitement.</i>
</b><br /><br />What I also enjoyed was that Kayla was no weakling next to Nick. She was able to fight her own fights and make him see things from her point of view. She also was able to tolerate the violent world Nick lives in and didn't have any hopes or dreams about ever leaving all of this behind. <br /><br />And they had super hot chemistry. The scenes where Nick was trying to seduce Kayla... HAWT! And when he fell in love with her... Aww... That was so sweet. He was suddenly so sweet and attentive and thoughtful. <br /><br />And he called her Princess... What more can you ask for? <br /><br /><b>Should you read it?</b> I don't even have words to tell you to go and read it right this moment. Just do yourself a favor and read it, now. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6973090125747154643" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_622278236" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/622278236" />
    <a title="Julie Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9597439-julie-reads"><img alt="Julie Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1494558964p2/9597439.jpg" /></a>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/622278236?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julie Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julie Reads" href="/user/show/9597439-julie-reads">Julie Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer622278236" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13970808883704134718">To be fair, my rating is only for first half of the book, I couldn't finish. Good premise, sloppy execution.<br/><br/>It just didn't work for me. The book felt rushed most of the time (first half I read, anyway) and the characters are so one dimensional, it's annoying!</span>

          </span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_50082241'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/50082241-collateral"><img alt="Collateral" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1568009091l/50082241._SX98_SY160_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('X6AZQM47QHyyeis6gpWKwCDC052FSZSIkvnuG6THcgc4aJfhWnmJW9FOGBUfwiUlYybQxLod5pzC68fZSCdDkA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9zwdzk3FpeaQBpJCi5xF22B3cN/Oo4jhM60ezcEE/eeQ9JNv2YdswfMyoW0Wy+o+I5NzhvH3+vVjvzcPLeTMcA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

With darkened tenacity, Savage has watched Nick since he was a child and has never given up on his pursuit of him. He will do anything to have Nick join him and become a part of his organization. Savage will even allow Brady Simone to pursue him for a time, without killing him. For the sake of his sister’s happiness protecting Brady is important but keeping Savage away from his sister is Nick’s primary goal. If Savage learns of Lena, she will instantly be marked for death. Nick has no choice but to meet Savage in his own territory and ask for a favor, something he has avoided at all costs until now. Their meeting is ominous. It brings back memories and rekindles Savage’s desire to have Nick take the place where his father once stood. Will Nick be allowed to decline Savage’s offer again? Or will Nick find killers on his heels, ready to take his place in Savage’s favor? Or will Savage simply kill everyone that gets in his way and replace his desire for Nick with the only one that can replace him - Nicky? \n\n“Savage’s voice cuts through my pain and releases me, allowing me to finally see again.
